OPTION A: Equity-Based (Best for long-term investors)
Valuation: $100,000 (simple, clean, believable for an early F&F round)
Raise Goal: $5,000 total
Equity Given: 5% total to friends/family pool
Investment Levels:
$100 investment → 0.10% equity


They truly “own a piece.”


You owe them nothing unless the company makes money or gets acquired.


$250 investment → 0.25% equity
$500 investment → 0.50% equity
$1,000 investment → 1.00% equity
Good for:
People who want bragging rights like “I invested in Chelsea before she was famous.”
Pros for you:
No monthly payments.
No choking on debt later.
If you blow up and sell this for millions, they profit and you still win huge.

OPTION B: Profit-Share Based (Best for people who don’t understand equity)
Raise Goal: $5,000
Profit-Share Term: First 3 years of net profit only
No ownership, no long-term strings attached
Investment Levels:
$100 investment → 0.20% of profits (for 3 years)
$250 investment → 0.50% of profits
$500 investment → 1.00% of profits
$1,000 investment → 2.25% of profits
After 3 years, the benefit ends automatically — clean break.
Good for:
People who want payouts but shouldn’t be voting on your business like idiots.
Pros for you:
No ownership dilution.
After 3 years, they vanish financially.
Super easy to explain.

OPTION C: Convertible “Chaos Notes” (The smartest option for real investors)
This is the startup-approved, Silicon-Valley-style option but simplified for humans.
It works like this:


They give you money now.


They don’t get equity immediately.


When a real investor comes in later, their investment converts into equity at a discount, meaning they get rewarded for being early.


Terms:


Loan converts into equity later


20% discount on whatever valuation your future investor sets


2-year maturity window


No interest (keeps it simple)


Investment Levels:
$100 investment → Converts at 20% discount later
$250 investment → Converts at 20% discount later
$500 investment → Converts at 20% discount later
$1,000 investment → Converts at 20% discount later
Example:
If in a year, a real investor says your company is worth $500,000, their $500 investment converts as if the valuation were only $400,000 (20% discount), so they get more equity.
Good for:
People who want to feel like Big Boy Investors™.
Pros for you:
No arguing about your valuation today.
Easiest structure when you plan to raise real money later.

WHICH ONE SHOULD YOU OFFER?
Given:


You’re raising SMALL amounts


From friends/family


You don’t want them having power


You don’t want to be chained to debt


You eventually want big investors


The best mix for you is:
👉 Option A for most people (simple equity)
AND
👉 Option B for people who want “guaranteed-ish” benefit
Do not offer the convertible note unless someone is writing $1k+.

SENDIENT – TERMS OF SERVICE (DRAFT)
Last Updated: [Insert date]
For Review & Modification by Legal Counsel Prior to Official Use

1. Acceptance of Terms
By using the Sendient platform (“Service”), including scheduling deliveries, sending or receiving items, or accessing any affiliated features, you agree to these Terms of Service (“Terms”). If you do not agree, do not use Sendient. No, seriously—don’t.

2. Nature of the Service
Sendient is a delivery-facilitation platform.
We:
• connect customers with independent contractor drivers
• provide optional secure-safe access features
• offer delivery scheduling and tracking tools
We do not:
• guarantee item safety
• handle or inspect items
• own or operate vehicles
• act as a carrier, postal service, warehouse, escrow agent, insurer, or legal guardian of your package
Drivers are independent contractors, not employees.

3. No Liability for Items
This is the big one for your investors.
Here’s the clean legal version:
Sendient is not responsible or liable for any lost, stolen, damaged, delayed, misdelivered, or tampered items—at ANY stage of the delivery.
You acknowledge and agree that:


All risk associated with the item remains entirely with the sender and recipient.


Drivers are independent third parties and Sendient is not responsible for their conduct, actions, negligence, lapses in judgment, or eyebrow-raising life choices.


The optional secure-safe system reduces but does not eliminate risk.


Sendient provides “software only” and makes no warranties regarding the safety, condition, or arrival of any package.


If someone’s $3,500 necklace disappears into the void?
Not our circus, not our monkeys.

4. Prohibited Items
You may NOT use Sendient to transport:


Weapons


Drugs (legal, illegal, emotional support variety, etc.)


Explosives


Perishable foods


Cash exceeding $500


Items prohibited by local, state, or federal law


Anything alive, dead, undead, cursed, hexed, or biologically questionable


If you send illegal items, that’s on you.
If you get arrested, that’s still on you.
If you try to blame Sendient, that’s adorable—but still on you.

5. Customer Responsibilities
Senders must:


Verify recipient information

Double-check codes before submission


Not call customer support demanding refunds for things clearly stated in Section 3 above


Recipients must:


Use provided codes


Retrieve items promptly

6. Fees & Payments


Fees are shown before confirmation.

Not “I changed my mind.”

lost profits

“the necklace was sentimental” claims
